<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QLDPC码的高速率和高距离特性使其成为可扩展量子计算的有前景候选，但设计低深度症状提取电路以避免钩错误（辅助量子比特错误传播到多个数据量子比特）非常困难，且基于置信传播的译码器受到Tanner图中短环的损害。

Method: 提出硬件感知方法：使用偏置噪声辅助量子比特（仅受相位翻转错误影响）来避免钩错误和短环。以自行车双变量码和循环超图积码为例，比较传统症状提取电路与使用偏置噪声辅助比特时的有效故障距离和短环数量。

Result: 当辅助比特仅受相位翻转错误（无比特翻转错误）时，有效故障距离显著提高，短环数量显著降低。在电路噪声2×10⁻³且辅助比特比特翻转错误率比相位翻转错误率低50倍时，逻辑错误率改善近一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了即使无法维持完全偏置，使用偏置噪声量子比特也能在量子纠错中带来显著且实用的优势。

Abstract: Remarkable technical progress has made high-rate, high-distance, quantum low-density parity-check codes (QLDPC) promising candidates for scalable quantum computing. However, it is hard to design low-depth syndrome extraction circuits that do not spread errors from ancilla qubits to multiple data qubits, also known as hook errors, for general QLDPC codes. Additionally, widely used decoders for these codes based on belief propagation are impaired due to short loops in the Tanner graph. Here, we investigate a hardware-aware approach to avoid these hooks and loops using biased noise ancillas. Using examples of bicycle bivariate codes and a cyclic hypergraph product code, which have been widely considered for practical application, we show that the effective fault-distance of the conventional syndrome extraction circuit can be significantly higher and the number of short loops can be significantly lower when the ancillas are subject to phase-flip errors only, compared to when they are also subject to bit-flip errors. This can result in almost an order of magnitude improvement in the logical error rate at circuit noise of $2\times 10^{-3}$ and when bit-flip errors in the ancilla are 50 times less likely than phase-flip errors. Our work demonstrates a significant and practical quantum error correction advantage with biased noise qubits in which full-bias cannot be maintained.

</details>


### [131] [Provably Efficient Learning of Fermionic Correlations under Particle-Number Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30601)
*Yuki Koizumi,Kaito Wada,Toshinori P. Takama,Nobuyuki Yoshioka*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于随机轨道旋转的粒子数守恒费米子阴影层析框架，证明可以用$O_k(\eta^k/\varepsilon^2)$个样本同时估计所有$k$体费米子关联，样本量不依赖于系统大小$N$，并建立了匹配的信息论下界，实现了粒子数对称性在费米子可观测量估计中的可证明高效优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子数对称性对量子态施加了强结构约束，但此前尚不清楚这种对称性是否能在集体学习局部关联中带来可证明的优势。作者希望建立一种理论框架来严格证明利用粒子数对称性可以显著降低样本复杂度。

Method: 提出基于随机轨道旋转的粒子数守恒费米子阴影层析框架。构造随机费米子高斯幺正变换，利用粒子数对称性设计测量协议；通过理论分析证明样本复杂度上界$O_k(\eta^k/\varepsilon^2)$；采用信息论方法证明匹配的下界$\Omega_k(\eta^k/\varepsilon^2)$；通过数值计算验证实际性能。

Result: 证明对于任意$k$体费米子关联，仅需$O_k(\eta^k/\varepsilon^2)$个样本即可达到方差$\varepsilon^2$，样本量完全独立于系统大小$N$；建立信息论下界$\Omega_k(\eta^k/\varepsilon^2)$，证明该依赖关系最优；数值实验表明，在$N=100,\eta=20,\varepsilon=10^{-2}$时，单体关联估计的查询数比最先进方法减少约一个数量级。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了粒子数对称性在费米子可观测量估计中的可证明高效优势，样本复杂度仅依赖于粒子数$\eta$和阶数$k$，与系统大小$N$无关，且上界与下界匹配表明该依赖关系在常数意义下最优。

Abstract: Predicting local fermionic correlations is a central task in quantum many-body physics, as these correlations encode many physically relevant local observables. The ubiquitous particle-number symmetry imposes strong structural constraints on quantum states, suggesting that local correlations should be learned with fewer samples than by symmetry-agnostic approaches. However, it has remained unclear whether such a provable advantage exists in collective learning of local correlations. Here, we develop a framework of number-conserving fermionic-shadow tomography based on random orbital rotations. We prove that, for every given order $k$, we can simultaneously estimate {\it all} $k$-body fermionic correlations of an $N$-mode $η$-particle state with a given variance $\varepsilon^2$ using only $O_k(η^k/\varepsilon^2)$ samples, which are independent of the system size $N$. We further establish a matching information-theoretic lower bound $Ω_k(η^k/\varepsilon^2)$ for any adaptive protocol based on single-copy measurements, showing that the $(η^k,\varepsilon)$-dependence is optimal up to constants depending only on $k$. Furthermore, our numerical calculation shows that the proposal reduces the query count by roughly an order of magnitude compared with state-of-the-art methods for one-body correlation estimation in a system of $N=100$, $η=20$ at $\varepsilon=10^{-2}$. This work establishes a provably efficient advantage of particle-number symmetry for fermionic observables estimation.

</details>


### [132] [Repetition-code-based readout error detection and correction across hardware platforms and generations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30606)
*Csaba Czabán,Orsolya Kálmán,Sergey N. Filippov,Zoltán Zimborás*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了重复码在量子处理器上用于读取错误检测与纠正的效果，发现该方法在所有测试设备上均能提升读取保真度，但其收益受硬件门错误率影响显著：超导处理器中编码引入的门错误限制了效果，而离子阱处理器因门错误率更低，更大码距仍能带来优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 读取错误是当前量子处理器的主要噪声源之一，影响期望值估计和采样应用。现有读取错误缓解技术只能纠正期望值等聚合量，无法对单次测量结果进行修正。因此需要一种能对单个测量shot进行修正的方法。

Method: 在测量前使用重复码将每个数据量子比特与辅助量子比特进行冗余编码，通过后选择或多数投票对测量结果进行解码。在IBM Heron r1-r3超导处理器和Quantinuum H1、H2离子阱处理器上跨平台、跨代际进行系统实验评估，独立变化码距、硬件代际和编码布局。

Result: 所有测试设备上，错误检测和纠正均提升了读取保真度，且即使未编码基线在硬件迭代中显著改善，提升依然存在。但额外冗余的价值强烈依赖于底层硬件：超导处理器上编码引入的门错误迅速抵消其收益，离子阱处理器因门错误率更低，更大码距仍保持优势。

Conclusion: 重复码读取错误检测与纠正方法有效，但效果受硬件门错误率制约。在门错误率较高的超导处理器上收益有限，在门错误率更低的离子阱处理器上更具优势。

Abstract: Readout errors are one of the dominant sources of noise in current quantum processors, limiting both expectation-value estimation and sampling-based applications. Since they affect only the classical measurement outcomes, they can be addressed using classical coding techniques: immediately before measurement, each data qubit is redundantly encoded with ancilla qubits, and the resulting bit string is decoded either by post-selection or by majority voting. Unlike conventional readout error mitigation, which corrects only aggregate quantities such as expectation values, this approach operates on individual measurement shots and can therefore produce approximately corrected samples. We present a systematic cross-platform and cross-generation experimental evaluation of repetition-code readout error detection and correction. We benchmark the same protocol on IBM Heron r1-r3 superconducting processors and Quantinuum H1 and H2 trapped-ion processors while independently varying the code distance, hardware generation, and encoding layout. We find that both error detection and correction improve readout fidelity on every device and generation tested, even as the unencoded baseline improves substantially across successive hardware releases. At the same time, the value of additional redundancy depends strongly on the underlying hardware. On superconducting processors, the extra gate errors introduced by the encoding rapidly offset its benefits, whereas on trapped-ion processors the much lower gate error rates allow larger code distances to remain advantageous.

</details>


### [133] [Provable random-matrix spectral ramp in a static, geometrically local Hamiltonian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30635)
*Matteo Ippoliti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在静态、几何局域的有限维量子多体系统中证明了谱型随机矩阵斜坡（ramp）的存在，通过将双酉Floquet电路的准能量谱嵌入到静态局域哈密顿量的能谱中，并证明其连接谱型因子继承了BKP斜坡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子混沌通常与随机矩阵统计相关，但此前仅在双酉Floquet电路中严格证明了谱型因子存在随机矩阵斜坡，静态局域哈密顿量中尚未有严格证明。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 基于Bertini-Kos-Prosen (BKP)的双酉电路结果，结合Feynman-Kitaev钟构造的变体，将双酉电路的Floquet准能量谱嵌入到一个静态局域哈密顿量的能量谱中，并证明后者的连接谱型因子在特定对称性扇区内继承了BKP斜坡。

Result: 在几何局域、有限局域希尔伯特空间维度的静态哈密顿量中，首次严格证明了谱型因子的随机矩阵斜坡行为。

Conclusion: 该工作是首个在时间无关、几何局域的多体系统中证明谱斜坡存在的严格结果，为理解静态系统中的量子混沌提供了重要理论依据。

Abstract: Quantum chaos is commonly associated with the emergence of random-matrix statistics in the spectra of quantum systems. A useful diagnostic is provided by the spectral form factor (SFF), which for random matrix ensembles displays a universal linear-growth regime (`ramp'). In the last decade, a landmark result by Bertini, Kos and Prosen (BKP) identified for the first time a class of geometrically local quantum dynamics of finite-dimensional particles where the SFF provably exhibits a random-matrix ramp: periodically driven (Floquet) qudit chains whose evolution is described by `dual-unitary' circuits. Here, building on the BKP result and on a recently proposed variant of the Feynman-Kitaev clock construction, we obtain a spectral ramp in a class of static, geometrically local Hamiltonians. Our strategy is to embed the Floquet quasienergy spectrum of a dual-unitary circuit into the energy spectrum of a static local Hamiltonian, and to prove that the latter's connected SFF inherits the BKP ramp within a symmetry sector. This is to our knowledge the first proof of a spectral ramp in a time-independent, geometrically local many-body system with finite local Hilbert space dimension.

</details>


### [134] [Authentication in Quantum Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30636)
*Christopher Battarbee,Suchetana Goswami,Elham Kashefi,Mina Doosti*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了量子通信中的认证问题，区分了经典消息认证、量子消息认证和实体认证三种类型，比较了代表性协议的安全性假设、设置需求、可组合性和可扩展性，并详细讨论了认证与量子密钥分发（QKD）及其他协议的关系。核心观点是：认证需求并非量子网络的固有局限，每个协议都依赖于特定的认证资源，安全声明只有在明确认证资源及其部署假设时才有意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子通信文献中常将不同类型的认证（经典消息认证、量子消息认证、实体认证）混为一谈，缺乏系统的比较和分类标准，导致协议选择和安全评估存在混乱。本文旨在厘清这些概念，建立清晰的比较框架，帮助研究者根据应用场景选择合适的认证方案。

Method: 采用综述性研究方法，对三类认证功能进行分类梳理，从安全性假设、设置需求、可组合性和可扩展性四个维度对代表性协议进行横向比较，并通过案例研究（QKD及其他协议）展示认证的实际应用场景。

Result: 1) 明确了三类认证功能（经典消息认证、量子消息认证、实体认证）的区别与联系；2) 基于比较标准识别并推荐了适用于不同场景的协议候选；3) 通过QKD案例展示了认证与密钥分发的依赖关系；4) 揭示了认证资源部署假设对协议安全声明的关键影响。

Conclusion: 认证需求不是量子网络的固有局限，而是与经典安全通信一样需要明确认证资源。现有的经典和量子文献已提供了多种量子安全的认证方案，关键在于根据功能需求、假设条件和安全保证进行精确匹配。协议的安全声明只有在认证资源及其部署假设被明确时才有意义。

Abstract: In this review, we survey the cryptographic task of authentication from the perspective of quantum communication. We review three main flavours of authentication that are often conflated in the literature: authentication of classical messages, authentication of quantum messages, and entity authentication, also covering recent hardware-assisted approaches. We compare representative protocols for each functionality in terms of their security assumptions, set-up requirements, composability, and scalability in large or dynamic networks, and use these criteria to identify and recommend suitable candidates. Finally, applications are surveyed: we provide a detailed case study of authentication and quantum key distribution (QKD), then extend the discussion to protocols beyond QKD, where the role of authentication is more complex. Our take-home message is that an authentication requirement is not an intrinsic limitation of quantum networks: as with all secure communication, each protocol relies on a particular authentication resource, and the security claim of that protocol is meaningful only once the authentication resource and its deployment assumptions are made explicit. At the same time, the existing classical and quantum literature already offers a range of quantum-secure authentication schemes, which can support different applications when carefully matched to the required functionality, assumptions, and security guarantees.

</details>
